              return new Promise(resolve => {
                  if (document.querySelectorAll(selector).length) {
                      return resolve(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
                  }
                  const observer = new MutationObserver(mutations => {
                      if (document.querySelectorAll(selector).length) {
                          resolve(document.querySelectorAll(selector));
                          observer.disconnect();
                      }
                  });
                  observer.observe(document.body, {
                      childList: true,
                      subtree: true
                  });
              });

fxvKED"><h2 class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 ixysCi">FAQs</h2></div><div class="style__Column-sc-1vzb2rb-0 fxvKED"><div class="Collapsible style__StyledItem-sc-ysddv3-3 hQAtNL"><button class="style__StyledTrigger-sc-ysddv3-4 gVCZQt"><h3 class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 jnNTpG">Who is Ro for?<span id="who-is-ro-for" aria-hidden="true" class="style__InvisibleAnchor-sc-ysddv3-7 lhjNJE"></span></h3><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="BaseIcon__SvgStyled-sc-1eh8j8p-0 qdHeg style__StyledAddNew-sc-ysddv3-2"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M11.25 12.75V21H12.75V12.75H21V11.25H12.75V3H11.25V11.25H3V12.75H11.25Z" fill="#1A1A1A"></path></svg></div></div></button><div id=":R5nacpri9H1:" class="Collapsible__contentOuter" style="height:0;-webkit-transition:height 200ms ease-out;-ms-transition:height 200ms ease-out;transition:height 200ms ease-out;overflow:hidden" role="region" aria-labelledby=":R5nacpri9:"><div class="Collapsible__contentInner"><div class="style__StyledContent-sc-ysddv3-5 dtqAa"><div class="style__ContentInnerWrapper-sc-ysddv3-6 MkfFp"><p class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 lghdVI">Ro is for adults who are experiencing health issues or want to improve or support their health and prefer to do so from the comfort of their home.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="Collapsible style__StyledItem-sc-ysddv3-3 hQAtNL"><button id=":R9nacpri9:" class="style__StyledTrigger-sc-ysddv3-4 gVCZQt"><h3 class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 jnNTpG">How does it work?<span id="how-does-it-work" aria-hidden="true" class="style__InvisibleAnchor-sc-ysddv3-7 lhjNJE"></span></h3><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="BaseIcon__SvgStyled-sc-1eh8j8p-0 qdHeg style__StyledAddNew-sc-ysddv3-2"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M11.25 12.75V21H12.75V12.75H21V11.25H12.75V3H11.25V11.25H3V12.75H11.25Z" fill="#1A1A1A"></path></svg></div></div></button><div id=":R9nacpri9H1:" class="Collapsible__contentOuter" style="height:0;-webkit-transition:height 200ms ease-out;-ms-transition:height 200ms class="style__ContentInnerWrapper-sc-ysddv3-6 MkfFp"><p class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 lghdVI">For prescription treatments, complete an online visit detailing your symptoms, health history, and goals. A US-licensed healthcare professional will review your information and make a personalized treatment recommendation. Ro will ship your treatment in discreet packaging with free shipping, if prescribed.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="Collapsible style__StyledItem-sc-ysddv3-3 hQAtNL"><button id=":Rdnacpri9:" class="Collapsible__trigger is-closed" aria-expanded="false" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls=":Rdnacpri9H1:" role="button"><div class="style__StyledHeader-sc-ysddv3-0 ivFSnT"><div class="style__StyledTrigger-sc-ysddv3-4 gVCZQt"><h3 class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 jnNTpG">Is my information safe?<span id="is-my-information-safe" aria-hidden="true" class="style__InvisibleAnchor-sc-ysddv3-7 lhjNJE"></span></h3><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="BaseIcon__SvgStyled-sc-1eh8j8p-0 qdHeg style__StyledAddNew-sc-ysddv3-2"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M11.25 12.75V21H12.75V12.75H21V11.25H12.75V3H11.25V11.25H3V12.75H11.25Z" fill="#1A1A1A"></path></svg></div></div></button><div id=":Rdnacpri9H1:" class="Collapsible__contentOuter" style="height:0;-webkit-transition:height 200ms ease-out;-ms-transition:height 200ms ease-out;transition:height 200ms ease-out;overflow:hidden" role="region" aria-labelledby=":Rdnacpri9:"><div class="Collapsible__contentInner"><div class="style__StyledContent-sc-ysddv3-5 dtqAa"><div class="style__ContentInnerWrapper-sc-ysddv3-6 MkfFp"><p class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 lghdVI">We take your privacy and the security of your information very seriously. We&#x27;ve designed the Ro platform to comply with all applicable privacy laws and have implemented a variety of technical and organizational security measures to protect your information against unauthorized disclosure or access.</p>
<p class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 lghdVI">Please read our <a node="[object Object]" class="style__NormalizedLink-sc-yq92gg-0 kPWoIT style__StyledLinkable-sc-1gl0kry-0 iblzCb" href="/privacy-policy">Privacy Policy</a> for more details about how we collect, use, and protect your data.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="Collapsible style__StyledItem-sc-ysddv3-3 hQAtNL"><button id=":Rhnacpri9:" class="Collapsible__trigger is-closed" aria-expanded="false" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls=":Rhnacpri9H1:" role="button"><div class="style__StyledHeader-sc-ysddv3-0 ivFSnT"><div class="style__StyledTrigger-sc-ysddv3-4 gVCZQt"><h3 class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 jnNTpG">Who are the healthcare professionals on the Ro platform?<span id="who-are-the-healthcare-professionals-on-the-ro-platform" aria-hidden="true" class="style__InvisibleAnchor-sc-ysddv3-7 lhjNJE"></span></h3><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="BaseIcon__SvgStyled-sc-1eh8j8p-0 qdHeg style__StyledAddNew-sc-ysddv3-2"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M11.25 12.75V21H12.75V12.75H21V11.25H12.75V3H11.25V11.25H3V12.75H11.25Z" fill="#1A1A1A"></path></svg></div></div></button><div id=":Rhnacpri9H1:" class="Collapsible__contentOuter" style="height:0;-webkit-transition:height 200ms ease-out;-ms-transition:height 200ms ease-out;transition:height 200ms ease-out;overflow:hidden" role="region" aria-labelledby=":Rhnacpri9:"><div class="Collapsible__contentInner"><div class="style__StyledContent-sc-ysddv3-5 dtqAa"><div class="style__ContentInnerWrapper-sc-ysddv3-6 MkfFp"><p class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 lghdVI">All of the doctors and nurse practitioners on the Ro platform are US-licensed healthcare professionals. Each doctor or nurse practitioner undergoes an extensive background check and license verification process.</p>
<p class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 lghdVI">When you message or talk with a doctor or nurse practitioner on the Ro platform, you can see their resume, medical license, and credentials any time you want. Just click on their name in the messaging thread in your account and take a look.</p>
<p class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 lghdVI">Ro also has a <a node="[object Object]" class="style__NormalizedLink-sc-yq92gg-0 kPWoIT style__StyledLinkable-sc-1gl0kry-0 iblzCb" href="/advisors">medical advisory board</a> that includes a former Surgeon General, world-renowned clinical directors, and medical leaders in fields including psychology, relationship counseling, men&#x27;s health, sexual health, neurology, pulmonology, male infertility, addiction, urology, pathology, and family medicine. Learn more about our medical advisory board <a node="[object Object]" class="style__NormalizedLink-sc-yq92gg-0 kPWoIT style__StyledLinkable-sc-1gl0kry-0 iblzCb" href="/advisors">here</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="style__Container-sc-2uwd8p-0 jClRcb"><div><h3 class="style__StyledParagraph-sc-143pjbh-0 eKuPwF">Still have questions?</h3><a
